  -ms-user-select: none;
  user-select: none;

  touch-action: pan-y;
  -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent;
}

  position: relative;
  overflow: hidden;
  display: block;
  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;
}

  outline: none;
}

  cursor: pointer;
  cursor: hand;
}

.slick-slider .slick-list {
  -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
  transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
}

  position: relative;
  left: 0;
  top: 0;
  display: block;
  margin-left: auto;
  margin-right: auto;
}

  content: "";
  display: table;
}

  clear: both;
}

  visibility: hidden;
}

  display: none;
}

}

}

}

}

}
